create table orders (
	orderkey			int,
	custkey			int 		unique,
	orderstatus		char(1),
	totalprice		float,
	clerk			char(15),
	comments		char(79)	 unique,
	primary key 		(orderkey)
 );
create index custkeyidx on orders (custkey);
create index commentsidx on orders (comments);
